***plas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plas.html>plas</a> (6666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plas.html>plas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plassen.html>plassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plasje.html>plasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a body of still water, pool
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plassen.html>plassen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:streek.html>streek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> turfwinning.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pools.html>pools</a></b> in this region result from the excavation of peat.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>puddle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>Om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plas.html>plas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloed.html>bloed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liep.html>liep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:raam.html>raam</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He walked around the <b>puddle</b> of blood towards the window.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> urine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>grote</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plas.html>plas</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He urinated extensively.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***plat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a> (2913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*plattus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_3">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">platter</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">platst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The world <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>of soft consistency
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:platte.html>platte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>soft</b> cheese (<a href = vnd.unilang:quark.html>quark</a>, creamy cheese)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Dutch Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Plat_(taal)" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Plat (taal)"><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>Plat</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Plat_(taal)" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Plat (taal)">Wikipedia <sup>nl</sup></a></span></div>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Platduits</i>, which originally referred to any dialect specific to the low countries.

***plataan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plataan.html>plataan</a> (114006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">platanus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">platane</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">platanus</i> but subsequently influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">platane</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πλᾰ́τᾰνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plátanos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which see.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:platbranden.html>platbranden</a> (16969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plat.html>plat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:branden.html>branden</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:platbranden.html>platbranden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to burn down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><small>(please add the primary text of this usage example)</small><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If your house <b>burned down</b> and you <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> nothing but the <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> on your back, what would you be worth to society and to yourself? How would you feel about losing all of the possessions you own? ― Winston Smith, "Why You Should Become a Minimalist"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***playboy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:playboy.html>playboy</a> (10759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">play</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boy</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:playboy.html>playboy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:playboys.html>playboys</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A single <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, especially a wealthy one, who devotes himself to a life of leisure and pleasure, often sexual, without commitments or responsibilities.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hedonist.html>hedonist</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***plechtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plechtig.html>plechtig</a> (11930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plichtich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plechtich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:plicht.html>plicht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>formal, stiff</li>

***plee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plee.html>plee</a> (6280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally part of a more elevated register, but shifted to colloquial or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> vulgar usage when <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wc.html>wc</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> into use. <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>Said</a> to derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">plaît-il</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plee.html>plee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plees.html>plees</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plee.html>pleetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:loo.html>loo</a>, john, bathroom
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wc.html>wc</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>May be considered inappropriate in formal <a href = vnd.unilang:settings.html>settings</a>. The word <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> however considered polite until the early twentieth century.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:informeel.html>informeel</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:spreektaal.html>spreektaal</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a> [1,2], <a href = vnd.unilang:wc.html>wc</a>

***plegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plegen.html>plegen</a> (2323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plien</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plēgen</i>, originally a class 4 strong verb. Presumably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*plian</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*plehaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to vouch for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. However, the form <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">plegan</i> already occurs in Old Dutch with <i>-g-</i>, and likewise for <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">plegan</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">pflegan</i>, so it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not certain what the exact relationship between the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plegen.html>plegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to do (something) habitually, customarily
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootvader.html>grootvader</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pleegt.html>pleegt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middageten.html>middageten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijp.html>pijp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roken.html>roken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My grandfather usually <a href = vnd.unilang:smokes.html>smokes</a> a pipe after <a href = vnd.unilang:lunch.html>lunch</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to usually happen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a> wandelvakanties <b><a href = vnd.unilang:placht.html>placht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regenen.html>regenen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">On our <a href = vnd.unilang:trekking.html>trekking</a> holidays, it often rained.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***plein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plein.html>plein</a> (7396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">plain</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">plānum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">level ground, a plain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pleh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Its use for "square" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an innovation, replacing <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plaetse</i> in standard language (compare dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></i>). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">plain</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">plane</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">chão</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">llano</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plein.html>plein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pleinen.html>pleinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pleintje.html>pleintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>square, plaza
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plein.html>plein</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dorp.html>dorp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onlangs.html>onlangs</a> heraangelegd <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> bloemenperken.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The square in our village <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> recently redone with new flowerbeds.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">binnenplein</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dorpsplein.html>dorpsplein</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marktplein.html>marktplein</a></span></li>

***plek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a> (517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">plecke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*plekka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mark, spot, place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*plakjō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spot, stain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">plecke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spot, mark</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pleck</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spot, place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at pleck.
</p>

***plengen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:plengen.html>plengen</a> (89290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:plengen.html>plengen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plengen.html>plengen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour, to cause to flow down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour on the ground or onto a cultic object as a sacrifice</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spill</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fling or hurl, to throw forcefully</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to insert with force</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plunge, to fall with noise</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rain hard</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to rain hard</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stortregenen.html>stortregenen</a></span></li></ul>
